| <span data-ttu-id="629fe-1056">Voce</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="629fe-1056">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="629fe-1057">Valore</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="629fe-1057">Value</span></span> |
